<DIV><FONT size="1" style="font-size:1pt;color:white">                 &#13;&#10;NEWS &#13;&#10; &#13;&#10; &#13;&#10;For news releases, related materials and high-resolution photos and video, visit www.media.ford.com.   &#13;&#10; &#13;&#10; &#13;&#10;www.twitter.com/ford &#13;&#10; &#13;&#10;www.facebook.com/ford &#13;&#10;Ford Names Lynn Vojvodich to Board of Directors &#13;&#10;DEARBORN, Mich., March 10, 2017 &#8211; Ford Motor Company (NYSE: F) is announcing today &#13;&#10;the election of Lynn Vojvodich to the company&#8217;s board of directors. Her appointment is effective &#13;&#10;April 1. &#13;&#10; &#13;&#10;Vojvodich, 49, is a global technology executive who has built, grown and transformed &#13;&#10;businesses for more than 20 years. She works with venture capital firms as an advisor to pre-&#13;&#10; IPO and start-up companies.  From 2013 to February 2017, Vojvodich was executive vice &#13;&#10;president and chief marketing officer of Salesforce, the world&#8217;s fourth largest enterprise software &#13;&#10;company and the global leader in customer relationship management. &#13;&#10; &#13;&#10;&#8220;Lynn is a proven marketing leader and entrepreneur with a wealth of experience in &#13;&#10;transforming customer relationships,&#8221; said Executive Chairman Bill Ford. &#8220;With deep &#13;&#10;experience, particularly in the software industry, she brings a unique perspective to the board &#13;&#10;that will help guide our strategy and evolving customer experience.&#8221;   &#13;&#10; &#13;&#10;Vojvodich will serve on the Ford Board of Directors&#8217; Nominating and Governance, Sustainability &#13;&#10;and Innovation, and Audit Committees.  &#13;&#10; &#13;&#10;Vojvodich has held leadership roles at Microsoft and BEA Systems and was a partner at the &#13;&#10;venture capital firm Andreessen Horowitz. She began her career as a mechanical engineer in a &#13;&#10;hard hat working on the design and construction of Gulfstream jets and offshore oil structures. &#13;&#10; &#13;&#10;Vojvodich serves as an independent director of The Priceline Group Inc. and was chairman of &#13;&#10;Take3, a marketing strategy firm she founded in 2006. She also has been recognized as one of &#13;&#10;Time&#8217;s Top 50 Women in Brand Marketing, Harvard Business School&#8217;s Most Inspiring Women in &#13;&#10;Silicon Valley and Ad Age&#8217;s Women to Watch.  &#13;&#10; &#13;&#10;She received a Bachelor of Science degree in Engineering and Product Design from Stanford &#13;&#10;University and a Master of Business Administration from Harvard Business School. &#13;&#10; &#13;&#10;Reference Information &#13;&#10; &#13;&#10;For biographical information and photos of Lynn Vojvodich, click here. &#13;&#10; &#13;&#10;# # # &#13;&#10;About Ford Motor Company &#13;&#10;Ford Motor Company is a global automotive and mobility company based in Dearborn, Michigan. With &#13;&#10;about 201,000 employees and 62 plants worldwide, the company&#8217;s core business includes designing, &#13;&#10;manufacturing, marketing and servicing a full line of Ford cars, trucks and SUVs, as well as Lincoln luxury &#13;&#10;vehicles. To expand its business model, Ford is aggressively pursuing emerging opportunities with &#13;&#10;investments in electrification, autonomy and mobility. Ford provides financial services through Ford Motor &#13;&#10;Credit Company. For more information regarding Ford and its products and services, please visit &#13;&#10;www.corporate.ford.com. &#13;&#10; &#13;&#10;Contacts: Susan Krusel     &#13;&#10; 313.322.7998 &#13;&#10;skrusel@ford.com &#13;&#10;   &#13;&#10; &#13;&#10;&#13;&#10;</FONT></DIV>
